# Description_Notes_and_Keywords
#   Description: This is an oak collection for the central part of Oland, a major island in the Baltic sea. A closer look at this collection reveals that it actually is in two parts. The younger consists mainly of samples collected from living trees in 2003-2005. Most of them only cover the 20th century, but a few goes back to mid 19th century. The other part is a selection among historical samples, 
# # almost all samples from postmills (small windmills), very typical for this island. NOAA Template Raw Measurements file added 2021-02-22.
